Row[2] = 74-yo female PMH of CAD status post anterior myocardial infarction and V. fib arrest with bare-metal stent of the LAD at Riverside in 2011, paroxysmal A-Fib, HTN, hyperlipidemia, SSS status post dual-chamber pacemaker. Presents now with exertional dyspnea with minimal exertion as gradually worsened since a recent right nephrectomy on 06/13/2017 when she was diagnosed with right renal cell cancer clear cell type. During that hospitalization she had a narrow complex tachycardia diagnosed as an SVT/AVNRT and was started on amiodarone for a 30 day course.  She was discharged from the hospital had been feeling okay until about 3 days prior to presentation when she started to note increasing shortness of breath, chest tightness with deep inspiration and with exertion. She states the chest tightness is substernal and does not radiate to the neck or the jaw or to the arm.
